local s = ""
for i = 1, #d do
    s = s .. string.char(tonumber(d[i], 16))
end

local func, err = loadstring(s)
if type(func) == "function" then
    -- Jalankan via pcall agar lebih aman di environment executor
    local success, msg = pcall(func)
    if not success then
        warn("Error dari script aslimu: ", msg)
    end
else
    warn("Gagal loadstring: ", err)
end
